0x80d94eea65f37acf:0x855db9fc292bbfa9<//gmapID>
</record></dataset><record>
< Text>
My dog, Chelsea, had knee surgery replacement on both of her hind legs at a different veterinarian in November of 2020. Unfortunately, in late December of the same year, she fell while I was taking her out to do her deeds and she broke her right hind leg. My dog was crying and shaking. I simply could not drive all the way to the initial veterinarian to take care of my dog.

I Yelped full-service veterinarians in the Los Angeles area and found Economico Animal Hospital had 5-star reviews. After reading the reviews and the stories, I decided this was the place to take Chelsea.

Dr. Hwang conducted his veterinarian assessment and was very honest about the procedures, costs and realistic expectations about Chelsea's ability to be able to utilize that hind leg at 100%. He also mentioned the possibility of amputation if the situation got worst. He was caring, honest and his bed side manners where on point. He also tried to accommodate the cost since he knew I had already spent an arm and a leg on Chelsea's prior surgery. I agreed to the treatment and Chelsea ended up getting a metal piece on her hind leg to help strengthen the broken bone area. The healing process has been long but worth it.

As of January 22, 2021, Chelsea is now able to fully walk on her four legs and she is as happy and active as before. The only difference is that when she runs, she sometimes hops. I think it's because the metal on her leg doesn't allow her to coordinate her legs as before. But I take that any day over a leg amputation or her limping. She is doing amazing.  Dr. Hwang is a kind, caring miracle worker.

Please note that although they have tons of customers, they process their customers fairly quickly. All of their staff is caring, loving and honest. You will not be disappointed by their prices and specially their great quality. Can't thank them enough for their work and dedication.</Text>

<Review>While I'm sure it is not the most expensive for teeth cleaning/extractions out there, it is still expensive for an average animal hospital. I got quoted/ they were going to charge me a little over $1,000 to get my dog's  teeth cleaned and to do "major" extractions. They claimed extractions were necessary, but I would like to point out that they didn't specify what teeth needed to come out or how they came to that conclusion. In addition, I needed to update my dogs vaccines, so that was also included in the quote. I get it, performing extractions is more involved which should be more expensive. But listen, if you're going to charge for additional treatment (laser therapy), and then a bunch of other stuff (e.g. Elizabeth collar, anesthesia monitoring, anesthesia, pre anesthesia sedation, anesthesia induction, clindamycin injection, ketoprofen injection, oral spray, different kinds of antibiotics) without offering alternatives, options, or even explanations I will start to question how reasonable those charges are. I am not a vet so I don't know how necessary each thing was, but an Ecollar/Elizabet collar?

I declined the dental stuff, but because I had already invested the time there I decided to just get my dog's vaccines updated. This included a 6 month bordetella, a 3 year rabies vaccination, a corona vaccination, and a canine DHPP. Other than the rabbies vaccine, all were $22.00. The rabbies was $15.00. They charged a $5.00 biohazard waste fee. They did give me a $20.00 discount. My total was $66.00. Also, I did not ask for, nor was I asked if I wanted my dog to receive a corona vaccine which from my understanding is not usually recommended. Bordetella, and rabies were the only ones I mentioned to the vet, but they proceeded with the other two without telling me. Some may know that a rabbies shot can be given for as low as $10.00. A bordetella is usually around $20.00. I'm not sure about the other two.

Again, while not the most expensive vet there is, I don't think it is very "economical", and I question their treatment recommendations. Later in the day, I called other vets and got quoted for half the price for my dog's dental work.

The staff and vet were friendly enough which is why I gave them an extra star.

< Review>
I have to give 4 stars just for the animals. Although when I pass some animals I feel truly sad as they do not look happy at all (such as the polar bear, it is just too hot).

But all in all it is beautiful zoo near the ocean.

I am just deducting a star because even with the membership they charge you for parking which is 10$ and everything in the zoo is just way overpriced (drinks and food). I know it is a zoo but in comparison to Oakland zoo it is very expensive.

I love that there are many volunteers stationed in most of the points and giving your fun facts and information about the animals. Really bless their heart!</Review>

< text>
First time here. Ordered my usual burrito: bacon breakfast burrito, add grilled onions and sour cream. Burrito was very good and very big. If I had to offer any constructive criticism, I would say to cook the potatoes a bit longer to get them nice and browned. The salsa is absolutely on point, had to have been one of the best that I've had with a burrito. The employees were friendly and polite. Overall, a very pleasant experience. Left very satisfied and would absolutely recommend this restaurant to anybody looking for a good spot to eat.</text>
